    <script>
        function showTab(tabName) {
            // ëª¨ë“  íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìˆ¨ê¸°ê¸°
            const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab');
            const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.content');
            
            tabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove('active'));
            contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
            
            // ì„ íƒí•œ íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  í™œì„±í™”
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

```markdown
# PRD (Product Requirements Document)

## Engineering Capability Growth Framework (ECGF)

---

## 1. ì œí’ˆ ê°œìš” (Overview)

### 1.1 ì œí’ˆëª…
**Engineering Capability Growth Framework (ECGF)**

### 1.2 ë°°ê²½

    <script>
        function showTab(tabName) {
            // ëª¨ë“  íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìˆ¨ê¸°ê¸°
            const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab');
            const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.content');
            
            tabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove('active'));
            contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
            
            // ì„ íƒí•œ íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  í™œì„±í™”
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function showTab(tabName) {
            // ëª¨ë“  íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìˆ¨ê¸°ê¸°
            const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab');
            const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.content');
            
            tabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove('active'));
            contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
            
            // ì„ íƒí•œ íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  í™œì„±í™”
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function showTab(tabName) {
            // ëª¨ë“  íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìˆ¨ê¸°ê¸°
            const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab');
            const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.content');
            
            tabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove('active'));
            contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
            
            // ì„ íƒí•œ íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  í™œì„±í™”
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                        <li>ì´ë¯¸ í•œ ë‹¨ê³„ ìœ„ ì—­í• ì„ í•˜ê³  ìˆëŠ”ê°€?</li>
                        <li>ì—†ì–´ì§€ë©´ ì¡°ì§ì´ í”ë“¤ë¦¬ëŠ” ê¸°ìˆ ì¸ê°€?</li>
                        <li>ì´ ì‚¬ëŒì´ í‚¤ìš´ ì‚¬ëŒì´ ìˆëŠ”ê°€?</li>

    <script>
        // ë¡œì»¬ ìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ì§€ì—ì„œ ë¶€ì„œì› ë°ì´í„° ê´€ë¦¬
        const STORAGE_KEY = 'ecgf_members';
        
        function getMembers() {
            const data = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
            return data ? JSON.parse(data) : [];
        }
        
        function saveMembers(members) {
            localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(members));
        }
        
        function showTab(tabName) {
            // ëª¨ë“  íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìˆ¨ê¸°ê¸°
            const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab');
            const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.content');
            
            tabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove('active'));
            contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
            
            // ì„ íƒí•œ íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  í™œì„±í™”
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
            
            // ë¶€ì„œì› ê´€ë¦¬ íƒ­ì¼ ê²½ìš° ëª©ë¡ ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨
            if (tabName === 'members') {
                renderMemberList();
            }
        }
        
        function saveMember(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            
            const members = getMembers();
            const editId = document.getElementById('editId').value;
            const memberData = {
                id: editId || Date.now().toString(),
                name: document.getElementById('memberName').value,
                primaryArchetype: document.getElementById('primaryArchetype').value,
                secondaryArchetype: document.getElementById('secondaryArchetype').value,
                years: parseInt(document.getElementById('years').value),
                level: document.getElementById('level').value
            };
            
            if (editId) {
                // ìˆ˜ì •
                const index = members.findIndex(m => m.id === editId);
                if (index !== -1) {
                    members[index] = memberData;
                }
            } else {
                // ì¶”ê°€
                members.push(memberData);
            }
            
            saveMembers(members);
            resetForm();
            renderMemberList();
        }
        
        function resetForm() {
            document.getElementById('memberForm').reset();
            document.getElementById('editId').value = '';
        }
        
        function editMember(id) {
            const members = getMembers();
            const member = members.find(m => m.id === id);
            
            if (member) {
                document.getElementById('editId').value = member.id;
                document.getElementById('memberName').value = member.name;
                document.getElementById('primaryArchetype').value = member.primaryArchetype;
                document.getElementById('secondaryArchetype').value = member.secondaryArchetype || '';
                document.getElementById('years').value = member.years;
                document.getElementById('level').value = member.level;
                
                // ë¶€ì„œì› ê´€ë¦¬ íƒ­ìœ¼ë¡œ ìŠ¤í¬ë¡¤
                document.getElementById('members').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
            }
        }
        
        function deleteMember(id) {
            if (confirm('ì •ë§ ì‚­ì œí•˜ì‹œê² ìŠµë‹ˆê¹Œ?')) {
                const members = getMembers();
                const filtered = members.filter(m => m.id !== id);
                saveMembers(filtered);
                renderMemberList();
            }
        }
        
        function renderMemberList() {
            const members = getMembers();
            const listContainer = document.getElementById('memberList');
            
            if (members.length === 0) {
                listContainer.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="empty-state">
                        <h3>ë“±ë¡ëœ ë¶€ì„œì›ì´ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤</h3>
                        <p>ìœ„ì˜ í¼ì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì—¬ ë¶€ì„œì›ì„ ë“±ë¡í•´ì£¼ì„¸ìš”.</p>
                    </div>
                `;
                return;
            }
            
            // ë ˆë²¨ë³„ë¡œ ì •ë ¬
            const levelOrder = { 'L1': 1, 'L2': 2, 'L3': 3, 'L4': 4, 'L5': 5 };
            members.sort((a, b) => {
                const levelDiff = (levelOrder[b.level] || 0) - (levelOrder[a.level] || 0);
                if (levelDiff !== 0) return levelDiff;
                return b.years - a.years;
            });
            
            listContainer.innerHTML = members.map(member => `
                <div class="member-card">
                    <div class="member-header">
                        <div class="member-name">${member.name}</div>
                        <div class="action-buttons">
                            <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-small" onclick="editMember('${member.id}')">ìˆ˜ì •</button>
                            <button class="btn btn-danger btn-small" onclick="deleteMember('${member.id}')">ì‚­ì œ</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="member-info">
                        <div class="info-item">
                            <span class="info-label">ì—…ë¬´ ë ˆë²¨:</span>
                            <span class="badge badge-level">${member.level}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="info-item">
                            <span class="info-label">ê·¼ë¬´ ì—°ì°¨:</span>
                            <span class="badge badge-years">${member.years}ë…„</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="info-item">
                            <span class="info-label">ì£¼ìš” ì„±í–¥:</span>
                            <span class="badge badge-archetype">${member.primaryArchetype}</span>
                        </div>
                        ${member.secondaryArchetype ? `
                        <div class="info-item">
                            <span class="info-label">ë³´ì¡° ì„±í–¥:</span>
                            <span class="badge badge-archetype">${member.secondaryArchetype}</span>
                        </div>
                        ` : ''}
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }
        
        // í˜ì´ì§€ ë¡œë“œ ì‹œ ë¶€ì„œì› ëª©ë¡ ë Œë”ë§
        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            renderMemberList();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>


```

```
engr/
â”œâ”€â”€ EngrSkill-Up.md          # PRD ë¬¸ì„œ
â”œâ”€â”€ README.md                 # í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ ê°œìš”

## 4. JavaScript ê¸°ëŠ¥

### 4.1 íƒ­ ì „í™˜ ê¸°ëŠ¥

#### í•¨ìˆ˜: `showTab(tabName)`
```javascript
function showTab(tabName) {
  // ëª¨ë“  íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìˆ¨ê¸°ê¸°
  const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab');
  const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.content');
  
  tabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove('active'));
  contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
  
  // ì„ íƒí•œ íƒ­ê³¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  í™œì„±í™”
  event.target.classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
  
  // ë¶€ì„œì› ê´€ë¦¬ íƒ­ì¼ ê²½ìš° ëª©ë¡ ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨
  if (tabName === 'members') {
    renderMemberList();
  }
}
```

### 4.2 ë¶€ì„œì› ê´€ë¦¬ ê¸°ëŠ¥

#### ë°ì´í„° ì €ì¥/ë¡œë“œ
```javascript
const STORAGE_KEY = 'ecgf_members';

function getMembers() {
  const data = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
  return data ? JSON.parse(data) : [];
}

function saveMembers(members) {
  localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(members));
}
```

#### ë¶€ì„œì› ë“±ë¡
```javascript
function saveMember(event) {
  event.preventDefault();
  
  const members = getMembers();
  const editId = document.getElementById('editId').value;
  const memberData = {
    id: editId || Date.now().toString(),
    name: document.getElementById('memberName').value,
    primaryArchetype: document.getElementById('primaryArchetype').value,
    secondaryArchetype: document.getElementById('secondaryArchetype').value,
    years: parseInt(document.getElementById('years').value),
    level: document.getElementById('level').value
  };
  
  if (editId) {
    // ìˆ˜ì •
    const index = members.findIndex(m => m.id === editId);
    if (index !== -1) {
      members[index] = memberData;
    }
  } else {
    // ì¶”ê°€
    members.push(memberData);
  }
  
  saveMembers(members);
  resetForm();
  renderMemberList();
}
```

#### ë¶€ì„œì› ëª©ë¡ ë Œë”ë§
```javascript
function renderMemberList() {
  const members = getMembers();
  const listContainer = document.getElementById('memberList');
  
  if (members.length === 0) {
    listContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">...</div>';
    return;
  }
  
  // ë ˆë²¨ë³„ë¡œ ì •ë ¬
  const levelOrder = { 'L1': 1, 'L2': 2, 'L3': 3, 'L4': 4, 'L5': 5 };
  members.sort((a, b) => {
    const levelDiff = (levelOrder[b.level] || 0) - (levelOrder[a.level] || 0);
    if (levelDiff !== 0) return levelDiff;
    return b.years - a.years;
  });
  
  listContainer.innerHTML = members.map(member => `
    <div class="member-card">
      <!-- ì¹´ë“œ ë‚´ìš© -->
    </div>
  `).join('');
}
```

#### ë¶€ì„œì› ìˆ˜ì •
```javascript
function editMember(id) {
  const members = getMembers();
  const member = members.find(m => m.id === id);
  
  if (member) {
    document.getElementById('editId').value = member.id;
    document.getElementById('memberName').value = member.name;
    // ... ë‚˜ë¨¸ì§€ í•„ë“œ ì±„ìš°ê¸°
  }
}
```

#### ë¶€ì„œì› ì‚­ì œ
```javascript
function deleteMember(id) {
  if (confirm('ì •ë§ ì‚­ì œí•˜ì‹œê² ìŠµë‹ˆê¹Œ?')) {
    const members = getMembers();
    const filtered = members.filter(m => m.id !== id);
    saveMembers(filtered);
    renderMemberList();
  }
}
```
